So, I want to know how to unstall the matlab from ubuntu or how to fix it?

### Post by monkeybrain20122 on 2014-04-05
To 'uninstall' just delete the MATLAB folder, that's it. So, say it is in /usr/local
```
sudo rm -r /usr/local/MATLAB
```

### Post by Rob Sayer on 2014-04-06
"I've tried to install matlab R2013a(Matlab801_MacUnix.iso)"

There is a linux version of that program.  I'm not surprised the Apple version doesn't work in ubuntu.

Using rm to uninstall is *not* the thing that'd pop to mind for me.  

I'd use synaptic personally or the terminal.  But I like the synaptic history/logs.  For newbies, software centre probably, but I'd recommend figuring out synaptic to them as well.

---

### Post by monkeybrain20122 on 2014-04-06
> **Rob Sayer said:**
> "I've tried to install matlab R2013a(Matlab801_MacUnix.iso)"



I think the 'MacUnix.iso' contains the installer for the Unix/Linux version. But you need an older gcc compiler to run your own codes (e.g gcc 4.4)
